## Attribution information

### Director(s)

[[Source]](https://starwars.fandom.com/wiki/Template:Movie)

:   "*There's been an awakening. Have you felt it?*"
:   ―Supreme Leader Snoke — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/62/AnAwakening.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250403184844)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:AnAwakening.flac "File:AnAwakening.flac"))[[1]](#cite_note-TFA-1)

***Star Wars*: Episode VII *The Force Awakens***, marketed as ***Star Wars: The Force Awakens***, is a [2015](/wiki/2015 "2015") film directed by [J.J. Abrams](/wiki/J.J._Abrams "J.J. Abrams"); co-written by Abrams, [Lawrence Kasdan](/wiki/Lawrence_Kasdan "Lawrence Kasdan"), and [Michael Arndt](/wiki/Michael_Arndt "Michael Arndt"); and produced by [Lucasfilm](/wiki/Lucasfilm "Lucasfilm") president [Kathleen Kennedy](/wiki/Kathleen_Kennedy "Kathleen Kennedy") and [Bad Robot Productions](/wiki/Bad_Robot_Productions "Bad Robot Productions"). It is the first part of the *[Star Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars "Star Wars")* [sequel trilogy](/wiki/Sequel_trilogy "Sequel trilogy"). The film stars [Harrison Ford](/wiki/Harrison_Ford "Harrison Ford"), [Mark Hamill](/wiki/Mark_Hamill "Mark Hamill"), [Carrie Fisher](/wiki/Carrie_Fisher "Carrie Fisher"), [Anthony Daniels](/wiki/Anthony_Daniels "Anthony Daniels"), and [Peter Mayhew](/wiki/Peter_Mayhew "Peter Mayhew") reprising their original roles. The original actors are joined by a host of new actors including [Daisy Ridley](/wiki/Daisy_Ridley "Daisy Ridley"), [John Boyega](/wiki/John_Boyega "John Boyega"), [Adam Driver](/wiki/Adam_Driver "Adam Driver"), and [Oscar Isaac](/wiki/Oscar_Isaac "Oscar Isaac").

The story begins thirty [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") after the events of [*Star Wars*: Episode VI *Return of the Jedi*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_VI_Return_of_the_Jedi "Star Wars: Episode VI Return of the Jedi"). The [First Order](/wiki/First_Order "First Order") has risen from the ashes of the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") and is opposed by [General](/wiki/General "General") [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo") and the [Resistance](/wiki/Resistance "Resistance"), both of which seek to find the missing [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker"). In the midst of this search, new heroes rise in the form of [Rey](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker"), a 19 year-old girl and a [Force-sensitive](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") [scavenger](/wiki/Scavenger "Scavenger") from [Jakku](/wiki/Jakku "Jakku"); [Finn](/wiki/Finn "Finn"), a [stormtrooper](/wiki/First_Order_stormtrooper "First Order stormtrooper") who defected from the First Order; and [Poe Dameron](/wiki/Poe_Dameron "Poe Dameron"), the best [pilot](/wiki/Pilot "Pilot") in the Resistance. They are aided by [Han Solo](/wiki/Han_Solo "Han Solo") in their search for Skywalker and their mission to destroy the First Order's new [superweapon](/wiki/Superweapon "Superweapon"), [Starkiller Base](/wiki/Starkiller_Base "Starkiller Base"), which targets the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic") and the Resistance for destruction. They are opposed by villains such as [Kylo Ren](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo"), a dark warrior with a mysterious past; and General [Armitage Hux](/wiki/Armitage_Hux "Armitage Hux"), the commander of Starkiller Base.

Despite initially claiming that the *Star Wars* story ended with the redemption of [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker") in *Return of the Jedi*, and after spending years refuting speculation that there would be another film, *Star Wars* creator [George Lucas](/wiki/George_Lucas "George Lucas") began work on Episode VII in [2011](/wiki/2011 "2011") in order to increase the value of Lucasfilm before he sold it to [The Walt Disney Company](/wiki/The_Walt_Disney_Company "The Walt Disney Company"), although Disney would later elect to not use Lucas' story. The acquisition was finalized on [October 30](/wiki/October_30 "October 30"), [2012](/wiki/2012 "2012"). Disney and Lucasfilm officially announced Episode VII and the sequel trilogy the same day. Lucasfilm later announced that the film would be an original story not beholden to the continuity of the *Star Wars* Expanded Universe, which was rebranded as the non-canon [*Star Wars* Legends](/wiki/Star_Wars_Legends "Star Wars Legends").

*The Force Awakens* was released on [December 17](/wiki/December_17 "December 17"), 2015 in the United Kingdom, Mexico, Latin America, and Asian countries; [December 18](/wiki/December_18 "December 18"), 2015 in North America; and [January 9](/wiki/January_9 "January 9"), [2016](/wiki/2016 "2016") in China. Some North American theaters offered special limited advance showings on the evening of December 17th rather than the traditional midnight showing. The film received widespread critical praise upon its release and was a massive box office success, becoming the highest grossing film of all time in North America when not adjusted for inflation. Worldwide, the film was the third highest-grossing film of all time at the time of its release (behind *Avatar* and *Titanic*). It is currently the sixth highest-grossing film of all time (behind *Avengers: Endgame*, *Avatar*, *Avatar: The Way of Water*, *Titanic*, and *Ne Zha 2*).

## Opening crawl[]

| Episode VII THE FORCE AWAKENS |
| --- |
| ``` Luke Skywalker has vanished. In his absence, the sinister FIRST ORDER has risen from the ashes of the Empire and will not rest until Skywalker, the last Jedi, has been destroyed.  With the support of the REPUBLIC, General Leia Organa leads a brave RESISTANCE. She is desperate to find her brother Luke and gain his help in restoring peace and justice to the galaxy.  Leia has sent her most daring pilot on a secret mission to Jakku, where an old ally has discovered a clue to Luke's whereabouts.... ``` |
|  |

## Plot summary[]

### [Attack on Tuanul](/wiki/Attack_on_Tuanul "Attack on Tuanul")[]

:   "*We got company.*"
:   ―Poe Dameron[[1]](#cite_note-TFA-1)

 [![ open fire on the village of Tuanul.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9e/Flametroopers_destroy_Tuanul.png/revision/latest?cb=20160414044547) [![ open fire on the village of Tuanul.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9e/Flametroopers_destroy_Tuanul.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160414044547)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9e/Flametroopers_destroy_Tuanul.png/revision/latest?cb=20160414044547) 

[Flametroopers](/wiki/First_Order_flametrooper "First Order flametrooper") open fire on the village of Tuanul.

 

Approximately 30 [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") after the [destruction of the second Death Star](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor"), [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker"), the last known surviving [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") has disappeared. Both the [First Order](/wiki/First_Order "First Order"), a successor to the fallen [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire"), and the [Resistance](/wiki/Resistance "Resistance"), a military force backed by the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic") led by Luke's twin sister, [General](/wiki/General "General") [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo"), [scour](/wiki/Hunt_for_Lor_San_Tekka "Hunt for Lor San Tekka") the galaxy in an attempt to find him.

Leia sends Resistance [pilot](/wiki/Resistance_pilot "Resistance pilot") [Poe Dameron](/wiki/Poe_Dameron "Poe Dameron") on a secret mission to the village of [Tuanul](/wiki/Tuanul "Tuanul") on the [desert](/wiki/Desert "Desert") [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") [Jakku](/wiki/Jakku "Jakku"), to meet with village elder [Lor San Tekka](/wiki/Lor_San_Tekka "Lor San Tekka"), who has obtained a [map](/wiki/Map_to_Skywalker "Map to Skywalker") to Luke Skywalker's location. During the meeting, First Order [stormtroopers](/wiki/First_Order_stormtrooper "First Order stormtrooper") under the command of [Kylo Ren](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo") and [Captain](/wiki/Captain "Captain") [Phasma](/wiki/Phasma "Phasma") attack the village. Poe and his [astromech droid](/wiki/Astromech_droid "Astromech droid") [BB-8](/wiki/BB-8 "BB-8") attempt to flee in their [T-70 X-wing starfighter](/wiki/Poe_Dameron%27s_blue_X-wing "Poe Dameron's blue X-wing"), but a pair of stormtroopers disable the [engines](/wiki/Engine "Engine") with their [blasters](/wiki/Blaster "Blaster"). With no alternative, Poe gives the map to BB-8 and orders the [BB unit](/wiki/BB-series_astromech_droid "BB-series astromech droid") to flee. Poe remains behind to cover BB-8's escape.

After stormtrooper [FN-2187](/wiki/Finn "Finn") is deployed, [FN-2003](/wiki/FN-2003 "FN-2003") is hit with blaster fire by Poe. FN-2187 goes to help his squadmate, but FN-2003's wound proves fatal, and in his final moments, FN-2003 smears his blood on FN-2187's helmet before dying, deeply affecting FN-2187. After securing the area, the remaining villagers are herded into the town square. Tekka is captured and brought before Kylo Ren, who demands to know where the map leading to Luke is. Tekka responds that he knows who Ren used to be, and chides Ren that he cannot escape his real identity. Growing impatient, Ren kills Tekka by striking him down with his [lightsaber](/wiki/Kylo_Ren%27s_lightsaber "Kylo Ren's lightsaber").

Poe takes a shot at Ren from cover, but Ren casually stops the blaster bolt in mid-air with [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force"). Poe is captured, and Ren decides to interrogate him further back on their ship. Before leaving, Phasma asks what to do with the crowd of captive villagers, and Ren orders them all slaughtered. Stormtrooper FN-2187 is horrified as the massacre plays out in front of him, remaining motionless and not firing his weapon.

### Return to the *Finalizer*[]

:   "*The Resistance will not be intimidated by you!*"
:   ―Poe Dameron to Kylo Ren[[1]](#cite_note-TFA-1)

 [![Kylo Ren probes Poe Dameron for information about the map.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b5/Kylo_tortures_Poe_Dameron.png/revision/latest?cb=20200624101324) [![Kylo Ren probes Poe Dameron for information about the map.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b5/Kylo_tortures_Poe_Dameron.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200624101324)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b5/Kylo_tortures_Poe_Dameron.png/revision/latest?cb=20200624101324) 

Kylo Ren probes Poe Dameron for information about the map.

 

Returning to the [*Resurgent*](/wiki/Resurgent-class_Star_Destroyer "Resurgent-class Star Destroyer")[-class Star Destroyer](/wiki/Resurgent-class_Star_Destroyer "Resurgent-class Star Destroyer") *[Finalizer](/wiki/Finalizer "Finalizer")*, FN-2187 is overwhelmed with emotions because of the death of his squadmate and the massacre of the villagers. He ducks inside an empty shuttle to take his helmet off, breathing heavily, but Phasma notices him and tells him to submit his blaster for inspection, having earlier noticed that he did not fire a shot. Knowing he would be punished and re-evaluated for not firing on the villagers, and with his faith in the First Order severely shaken, he decides to desert. Meanwhile, after failed attempts of torturing Poe for vital information about the map of Luke Skywalker's location, Ren uses his [mind probe](/wiki/Mind_probe_(Force_power) "Mind probe (Force power)") Force power to pry the information from Poe's mind. Ren learns that the map is located within a BB series droid that fled the village, and informs General [Armitage Hux](/wiki/Armitage_Hux "Armitage Hux") of the new information.

### Encounter with the scavenger[]

:   "*Classified. Really? Me too. Big secret.*"
:   ―Rey to BB-8[[1]](#cite_note-TFA-1)

 [![Rey encounters BB-8 in the deserts of Jakku.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3f/Rey_encounters_BB-8_Ver2.png/revision/latest?cb=20191005120914) [![Rey encounters BB-8 in the deserts of Jakku.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3f/Rey_encounters_BB-8_Ver2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20191005120914)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3f/Rey_encounters_BB-8_Ver2.png/revision/latest?cb=20191005120914) 

Rey encounters BB-8 in the deserts of Jakku.

 

Elsewhere on Jakku, a [scavenger](/wiki/Scavenger "Scavenger") named [Rey](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker") traverses the corridors of a downed [*Imperial*-class Star Destroyer](/wiki/Imperial-class_Star_Destroyer "Imperial-class Star Destroyer") at the [Graveyard of Giants](/wiki/Starship_Graveyard "Starship Graveyard"). Scavenging through the Imperial Star Destroyer, she finds a valuable piece of salvage and drops it in her satchel. Rey heads to [Niima Outpost](/wiki/Niima_Outpost "Niima Outpost"), and hauls the sack of salvage throughout the town. She then goes to [Unkar Plutt](/wiki/Unkar_Plutt "Unkar Plutt") to exchange her scraps for [foodstuff](/wiki/Foodstuff "Foodstuff"), and he offers her a quarter portion for her salvage. After taking the foodstuff, Rey heads to her home, a downed [AT-AT](/wiki/All_Terrain_Armored_Transport "All Terrain Armored Transport"), and prepares a meal for herself. After finishing her meal, she watches a [starship](/wiki/Starship "Starship") depart from the planet and then notices a distant sound. She immediately runs off with her [quarterstaff](/wiki/Quarterstaff "Quarterstaff") to investigate.

There, she encounters BB-8 struggling against being captured by a [green-skinned](/wiki/Color "Color") [humanoid](/wiki/Humanoid "Humanoid") scavenger named [Teedo](/wiki/Teedo_(Niima_Outpost) "Teedo (Niima Outpost)"). She frees the [droid](/wiki/Droid "Droid") and gives it directions to Niima Outpost and sends it on its way, but BB-8 insists on traveling with her. Rey goes to Unkar Plutt to again exchange her salvage for foodstuff, and the [Crolute](/wiki/Crolute "Crolute") offers to buy BB-8 for sixty food portions; while tempted, Rey declines the offer. Plutt then sends two thugs to steal BB-8.

### Escape from the *Finalizer*[]

:   "*You do exactly as I say and I can get you out of here.*"
:   ―FN-2187 to Poe Dameron[[1]](#cite_note-TFA-1)

 [![FN-2187 and Poe Dameron walk through the halls of the Finalizer to escape.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/52/Finn_and_Poe_Escape_Finalizer.png/revision/latest?cb=20160403052456) [![FN-2187 and Poe Dameron walk through the halls of the Finalizer to escape.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/52/Finn_and_Poe_Escape_Finalizer.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160403052456)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/52/Finn_and_Poe_Escape_Finalizer.png/revision/latest?cb=20160403052456) 

FN-2187 and Poe Dameron walk through the halls of the *Finalizer* to escape.

 

Needing a pilot to escape, FN-2187 frees the captured Poe Dameron from his cell, and the two steal a [TIE/sf fighter](/wiki/Unidentified_TIE/sf_space_superiority_fighter_(Finalizer) "Unidentified TIE/sf space superiority fighter (Finalizer)"). FN-2187 mans the guns, killing several of his former comrades in the hangar, and then disables the *Finalizer*'s [turbolasers](/wiki/Turbolaser "Turbolaser") on the outside of the vessel. During the escape, Dameron asks the stormtrooper his name, to which he explains that he has been raised from birth to be a stormtrooper, and the serial number "FN-2187" is the only designation he has ever had. Not content with calling a man a number, Dameron names the trooper "Finn", from the FN in his name. Finn likes the name, and goes on to use it. Dameron also tells him that the map vital to the Resistance was located within his astromech droid. Before they can continue their conversation and escape, the TIE is hit by a missile fired from the *Finalizer*, sending it spiraling towards the planet below.

Phasma reveals to Hux that this was FN-2187's first offense of non-conformity. A technician then informs Hux that the TIE fighter was projected to crash on [Goazon Badlands](/wiki/Goazon_Badlands "Goazon Badlands"), a canyon zone on Jakku. Realizing that Poe and Finn were going after BB-8, Hux sends out a squadron of search teams to the area.

### [Escape from Jakku](/wiki/Escape_from_Jakku "Escape from Jakku")[]

:   "*"What about that ship?"  
    "That one's garbage!"*"
:   ―Finn and Rey about the *Millennium Falcon*[[1]](#cite_note-TFA-1)

 [![Finn and Rey observe nearby Stormtroopers that are looking for BB-8.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d4/Finn_and_Rey_Jakku_Escape.png/revision/latest?cb=20160403053323) [![Finn and Rey observe nearby Stormtroopers that are looking for BB-8.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d4/Finn_and_Rey_Jakku_Escape.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160403053323)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d4/Finn_and_Rey_Jakku_Escape.png/revision/latest?cb=20160403053323) 

Finn and Rey observe nearby Stormtroopers that are looking for BB-8.

 

Finn and Dameron eject from the TIE shortly before it crashes, each landing separately some distance from the wreckage. Making his way to the crash, Finn finds Poe's [jacket](/wiki/Resistance_fighter_jacket "Resistance fighter jacket"), but no other sign of the man, and the fighter sinks into the sand. Believing Dameron to be dead, Finn begins wandering through the desert, discarding his stormtrooper armor along the way and eventually arriving at the nearest settlement, thirsting for water.

While Finn staggers to an animal trough to desperately slake his thirst, he notices thugs attempting to steal a BB unit droid, which Finn recognizes as BB-8, from a woman, Rey, but she fends them off with her staff. BB-8 notices Finn, wearing his master Dameron's jacket, prompting Rey to chase after him. Rey attacks Finn, believing him to be a thief. Finn explains that he had met and helped Poe escape the Resurgent Star Destroyer, but that Dameron had apparently perished during their crash. The First Order tracks Finn to the settlement, and launches an airstrike in attempt to search for BB-8 and the map. Rey, Finn, and BB-8 attempt to flee towards a [Quadjumper](/wiki/TUG-b13 "TUG-b13"), but [TIE/fo fighters](/wiki/TIE/fo_space_superiority_fighter "TIE/fo space superiority fighter") destroy it. With only one option left, the trio manages to escape in the *[Millennium Falcon](/wiki/Millennium_Falcon "Millennium Falcon")*. Rey flies it through the Graveyard of Giants, while Finn fires on and destroys the pursuing TIE fighters. With the TIE fighters destroyed, they escape into space.

Back aboard the *Finalizer*, Lieutenant [Dopheld Mitaka](/wiki/Dopheld_Mitaka "Dopheld Mitaka") informs Kylo Ren that the droid escaped on a stolen freighter and that it was aided by the deserter FN-2187. Ren activates his lightsaber and lashes out in a rage-fueled tantrum, slashing at an instrument panel uncontrollably. Mitaka tells Ren that they also appear to have been helped by a local scavenger girl. Kylo grows even more livid, using the Force to pull the officer by his throat across the room in order to choke him with his bare hands, and asking him what girl it was.

### Reunited with the *Falcon*[]

:   "*Chewie, we're home.*"
:   ―Han Solo to Chewbacca[[1]](#cite_note-TFA-1)

 [![Han and Chewie are reunited with the Millennium Falcon once again.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/72/HanandChewie-TFA.png/revision/latest?cb=20200624102523) [![Han and Chewie are reunited with the Millennium Falcon once again.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/72/HanandChewie-TFA.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200624102523)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/72/HanandChewie-TFA.png/revision/latest?cb=20200624102523) 

Han and Chewie are reunited with the *Millennium Falcon* once again.

 

While Finn and Rey celebrate their escape from Jakku, the *Millennium Falcon* breaks down. The ship is in major need of repairs, so Finn, Rey and BB-8 begin working to fix it. While they are working on repairs, the ship is caught in a [tractor beam](/wiki/Tractor_beam "Tractor beam") by a freighter. Although they initially believe themselves to be captured by the First Order, they soon meet their real captors: [Han Solo](/wiki/Han_Solo "Han Solo") and [Chewbacca](/wiki/Chewbacca "Chewbacca"), the former owners of the ship. Upon boarding their old vessel, Han and Chewie go about inspecting their ship and find the two stowaways, Rey and Finn, who he assumes were the thieves that had stolen the *Falcon*. When Rey and Finn explain that they were going to take a droid named BB-8 to the Resistance because it has a map that would reveal Luke's location, Han and Chewie agree to help them.

### [Skirmish aboard the *Eravana*](/wiki/Skirmish_aboard_the_Eravana "Skirmish aboard the Eravana")[]

:   "*Your game is old. There's no one in the galaxy left for you to swindle.*"
:   ―Bala-Tik to Han Solo[[1]](#cite_note-TFA-1)

 [![Han attempts to talk his way out of a confrontation between two gangs.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/95/Han_and_Chewie_Eravana.png/revision/latest?cb=20160425031756) [![Han attempts to talk his way out of a confrontation between two gangs.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/95/Han_and_Chewie_Eravana.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160425031756)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/95/Han_and_Chewie_Eravana.png/revision/latest?cb=20160425031756) 

Han attempts to talk his way out of a confrontation between two gangs.

 

Unfortunately, Han's freighter, the *[Eravana](/wiki/Eravana "Eravana")*, is boarded by two notorious criminal factions, the [Guavian Death Gang](/wiki/Guavian_Death_Gang "Guavian Death Gang") and [Kanjiklub](/wiki/Kanjiklub "Kanjiklub"), both of whom want their money back from Solo. Not wanting Rey and Finn to be involved, Han hides both of them in the lower corridors of the freighter while he and Chewie go meet with the criminals, with BB-8 accompanying them. Han tries but fails to convince both parties that he would fix things eventually, with the Guavian Death Gang negotiator, [Bala-Tik](/wiki/Bala-Tik "Bala-Tik"), recognizing the BB-8 astromech droid from a First Order bounty placed on it. They demand that Han hand over the droid and any stowaways he might have on board. As the scuffle continues, Rey accidentally releases three [rathtars](/wiki/Rathtar "Rathtar"). The rathtars provide a distraction for Han and Chewie to escape, but one catches Finn and drags him around the freighter. Rey finds a control panel and shuts a blast door on the rathtar, freeing Finn. The two join Han and Chewie and successfully jump to [hyperspace](/wiki/Hyperspace "Hyperspace") in the *Falcon*. Bala-Tik then orders his men to inform the First Order that Han Solo and the BB unit are aboard the ship.

### Meeting with the Supreme Leader[]

:   "*Our strategy must now change.*"
:   ―Snoke to General Armitage Hux[[1]](#cite_note-TFA-1)

 [![Kylo Ren and Supreme Leader Snoke discuss the recent turn of events.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f5/Kylo_Ren_and_Snoke.png/revision/latest?cb=20200624101847) [![Kylo Ren and Supreme Leader Snoke discuss the recent turn of events.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f5/Kylo_Ren_and_Snoke.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200624101847)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f5/Kylo_Ren_and_Snoke.png/revision/latest?cb=20200624101847) 

Kylo Ren and Supreme Leader Snoke discuss the recent turn of events.

 

At [Starkiller Base](/wiki/Starkiller_Base "Starkiller Base"), a planet converted into a [superweapon](/wiki/Superweapon "Superweapon"), powered by draining the energy of a star, and capable of destroying star systems, Kylo Ren and General Hux are summoned by [Supreme Leader](/wiki/Supreme_Leader "Supreme Leader") [Snoke](/wiki/Snoke "Snoke"), who appears as a large remote [hologram](/wiki/Hologram "Hologram") projection. Hux suggests using the Starkiller superweapon to destroy the government of the New Republic and the Resistance, and Snoke grants him the permission to do so. Snoke reveals to Ren that the astromech droid containing the map now resides in the *Millennium Falcon* - along with his father, Han Solo. Ren insists that his father means nothing to him, and with Snoke's training, he would not be seduced to the [light side of the Force](/wiki/Light_side_of_the_Force "Light side of the Force").

### Journey to Takodana[]

:   "*Want to get BB-8 to the Resistance? Maz Kanata is our best bet.*"
:   ―Han Solo to Finn and Rey[[1]](#cite_note-TFA-1)

 [![Han, Rey, Finn, and BB-8 arrive at Maz Kanata's castle.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d5/Maz_Kanatas_Castle_Takodana.png/revision/latest?cb=20160403173505) [![Han, Rey, Finn, and BB-8 arrive at Maz Kanata's castle.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d5/Maz_Kanatas_Castle_Takodana.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160403173505)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d5/Maz_Kanatas_Castle_Takodana.png/revision/latest?cb=20160403173505) 

Han, Rey, Finn, and BB-8 arrive at Maz Kanata's castle.

 

During the travel in hyperspace, the *Falcon* experiences a problem with its hyperdrive, but Rey demonstrates her knowledge of ships by bypassing the compressor and fixing the issue. Meanwhile, Finn attempts to bandage Chewie's arm, which was wounded while fighting on the *Eravana*. After fixing the ship, Han questions Finn and Rey, wondering why they are fugitives. Rey explains that the First Order is after the map located within BB-8 and that Finn is with the Resistance.

After BB-8 displays a projection of the map, Han explains that after Luke disappeared, there were many parties that went searching for him. Luke had tried to rebuild the Jedi Order, but an apprentice of his turned to the dark side, destroying all that Luke had built and killing the other [padawans](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") that Luke had trained. Feeling responsible and blaming himself for the failure, Luke went into exile. Han also explains that he heard rumors that Luke went searching for the [first Jedi Temple](/wiki/First_Jedi_Temple "First Jedi Temple").

Solo explains that he was able to find the *Millennium Falcon* soon after it entered space because he and Chewbacca were scanning for its signature. This was also why the criminal gangs were able to track it down so quickly, and meant the First Order could track it as well. In order to bring BB-8 to the Resistance, they needed to switch to a clean ship, which Han says he can obtain from an old friend.

Solo takes Rey, Finn, and BB-8 to the planet [Takodana](/wiki/Takodana "Takodana") to meet with [Maz Kanata](/wiki/Maz_Kanata "Maz Kanata") at her [castle](/wiki/Takodana_Castle "Takodana Castle"). Han says that she has maintained her castle for over a thousand years, where she runs a bustling cantina. Unbeknownst to all, spies from different sides take notice of the group. [GA-97](/wiki/GA-97 "GA-97") alerts the Resistance that the BB unit has been located, while [Bazine Netal](/wiki/Bazine_Netal "Bazine Netal") informs the First Order of the same.

### The conflict within[]

:   "*Forgive me. I feel it again... the pull to the light. Supreme Leader senses it. Show me again, the power of the darkness, and I will let nothing stand in our way. Show me, Grandfather, and I will finish what you started.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren to Darth Vader's helmet — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8a/ThePullToTheLight.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250403184900)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:ThePullToTheLight.flac "File:ThePullToTheLight.flac"))[[1]](#cite_note-TFA-1)

 [![Kylo Ren seeks guidance from his grandfather, Darth Vader.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/79/Kylo_Ren_Vader_Helmet_Chamber.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160420020932) [![Kylo Ren seeks guidance from his grandfather, Darth Vader.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/79/Kylo_Ren_Vader_Helmet_Chamber.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160420020932)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/79/Kylo_Ren_Vader_Helmet_Chamber.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160420020932) 

Kylo Ren seeks guidance from his grandfather, Darth Vader.

 

Attempting to seek guidance from his grandfather, [Darth Vader](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"), Kylo Ren sits quietly in his meditation chamber. In front of him is the burned helmet of Vader, recovered from the funeral pyre on [Endor](/wiki/Endor "Endor"). With the re-emergence of his father and Snoke's orders to kill him, Kylo feels an internal struggle within himself. He reveals to Vader's burned helmet that the light is pulling him in again and that even Snoke could sense it. He then asks his grandfather to show him the power of the darkness again, to pull him back to the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force") and help him overcome his future trials.

### A call from the Force[]

:   "*Rey... these are your first steps.*"
:   ―The voice of [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi") during Rey's vision[[1]](#cite_note-TFA-1)

Han and Chewie speak with Maz. Finn arranges with [Sidon Ithano](/wiki/Sidon_Ithano "Sidon Ithano") and his first mate [Quiggold](/wiki/Quiggold "Quiggold") that he will work as payment if they will fly him to the [Outer Rim](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories"). Rey implores Finn not to leave, but instead to help her find the Resistance. Finn, however, insists on leaving, and that there is no way to defeat the First Order. He also admits that he lied about being in the Resistance. He tells his story that he was a stormtrooper in the First Order. He had deserted after his first battle because he didn't want to kill unarmed villagers, for the First Order.

After Finn leaves, Rey hears the screaming of a young girl. She follows the screams. She descends deeper and enters a chamber that contains many relics from the past. The Force calls her to Maz's curio box, an ancient [*Wroshyr* wood](/wiki/Wroshyr_wood "Wroshyr wood") chest. Inside it, she finds the [lightsaber](/wiki/Skywalker_lightsaber "Skywalker lightsaber") that had previously belonged to Anakin Skywalker and his son Luke.

 [![Luke Skywalker and R2-D2 as seen in Rey's Force vision.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/de/Force_Vision_of_Jedi_Massacre_TFA.png/revision/latest?cb=20160416235713) [![Luke Skywalker and R2-D2 as seen in Rey's Force vision.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/de/Force_Vision_of_Jedi_Massacre_TFA.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160416235713)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/de/Force_Vision_of_Jedi_Massacre_TFA.png/revision/latest?cb=20160416235713) 

Luke Skywalker and R2-D2 as seen in Rey's Force vision.

 

Upon touching the lightsaber, she receives a series of [visions](/wiki/Force_vision "Force vision"). Rey sees [Cloud City](/wiki/Cloud_City "Cloud City") and sees that there [Luke duelled Darth Vader](/wiki/Duel_on_Cloud_City "Duel on Cloud City"). She sees Luke placing his metallic hand on top of [R2-D2](/wiki/R2-D2 "R2-D2") near a fire, (presumed to be Luke's burning [Jedi temple](/wiki/Jedi_Temple_of_Luke_Skywalker "Jedi Temple of Luke Skywalker")). Next, she is lying on the ground, in the rain at night. Corpses lay around the [Knights of Ren](/wiki/Knights_of_Ren "Knights of Ren") who slaughtered these victims. Kylo Ren notices and comes toward her. Before he reaches her, she sees herself as a child yelling, to her parents to stay on Jakku. When her parents were leaving Jakku, Unkar Plutt told her to quiet herself. Next, she sees Ren is chasing her in a snowy forest, in the future. Rey pulls herself out of the vision in terror. After the vision, she finds Kanata standing outside the room. Kanata explains to her the lightsaber's history and that it was calling to her. Kanata then reveals that she herself is Force-sensitive; although she was never a Jedi, she can simply close her eyes and feel the light of the Force within herself, and recognizes that Rey can do this too. Frightened by her vision, Rey runs into the woods with BB-8.

### [Hosnian Cataclysm](/wiki/Hosnian_Cataclysm "Hosnian Cataclysm")[]

:   "*Today is the end of the Republic! The end of a regime that acquiesces to disorder!*"
:   ―General Armitage Hux[[1]](#cite_note-TFA-1)

 [![General Hux commands the firing of the Starkiller superweapon.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Hux_and_Starkiller_Base.png/revision/latest?cb=20160425032958) [![General Hux commands the firing of the Starkiller superweapon.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Hux_and_Starkiller_Base.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160425032958)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Hux_and_Starkiller_Base.png/revision/latest?cb=20160425032958) 

General Hux commands the firing of the Starkiller superweapon.

 

After gaining Supreme Leader Snoke's permission to fire the Starkiller superweapon, Hux chooses the [Hosnian system](/wiki/Hosnian_system "Hosnian system"), which hosts the capital of the New Republic, [Hosnian Prime](/wiki/Hosnian_Prime "Hosnian Prime"), as well as the [New Republic Defense Fleet](/wiki/New_Republic_Defense_Fleet "New Republic Defense Fleet"), in order to demonstrate the power of the First Order in an attempt to wipe out the "illegitimate" government of the New Republic in one fell swoop. The test is a success and Hosnian Prime, the current elected home of the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/New_Republic_Senate "New Republic Senate"), all other astronomical bodies in the system, and an unknown percentage of the New Republic fleet are annihilated by the First Order's superweapon. The destruction of the Hosnian system is visible from the surface of Takodana. Shaken by the destruction, Finn re-evaluates his choice to leave.

### [Battle of Takodana](/wiki/Battle_of_Takodana "Battle of Takodana")[]

:   "*I need a weapon!*"  
    "*You have one!*"
:   ―Finn and Maz Kanata[[1]](#cite_note-TFA-1)

 [![Rey watches as Maz Kanata's castle is fired upon by the First Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7a/Pirate_castle_sacked.png/revision/latest?cb=20160425033805) [![Rey watches as Maz Kanata's castle is fired upon by the First Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7a/Pirate_castle_sacked.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160425033805)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7a/Pirate_castle_sacked.png/revision/latest?cb=20160425033805) 

Rey watches as Maz Kanata's castle is fired upon by the First Order.

 

The First Order, tipped off to BB-8's presence, arrives and attacks Maz Kanata's castle. Flying in with TIE fighters and [Atmospheric Assault Landers](/wiki/AAL-1971/9.1_Troop_Transport "AAL-1971/9.1 Troop Transport"), the First Order swiftly assaults the castle and levels it, killing many of its inhabitants. Maz gives Luke's old lightsaber to Finn for safekeeping, telling Han she doesn't have time to tell him how she retrieved it. BB-8 follows Rey into the forests surrounding the castle, and the First Order is unable to locate the droid until a stormtrooper officer reports to Kylo Ren that the astromech had been sighted in the company of a girl.

During the fighting at the castle, Finn wields the lightsaber to kill one stormtrooper before he is overpowered by [FN-2199](/wiki/FN-2199 "FN-2199"), a former squadmate of Finn's. His life is narrowly saved by Han, who uses Chewbacca's bowcaster to blast FN-2199 at the last second. Han and Chewbacca also kill multiple stormtroopers, but are captured along with Finn by the First Order. However, Resistance T-70 X-wings led by Poe Dameron, who is now revealed to still be alive, arrive to fight the First Order. A fierce dogfight ensues and results in the destruction of many First Order TIE fighters and the deaths of many stormtroopers from X-wing strafing runs.

Rey encounters Kylo Ren at the woods, and fires at him with her blaster pistol, but Kylo restrains her using the Force. Probing her mind, he discovers that she has seen the map he's been looking for all this time, and orders the First Order to pull out, saying they had what they came for and no longer need BB-8. As the battle rages on above the castle, the remaining First Order troops board their ships and retreat, and Han witnesses his son carrying an unconscious Rey away. The Resistance is victorious, freeing Finn, Han, and Chewbacca. Han and Leia are reunited, and Han reveals to Leia that he saw their son.

### Reunited at the Resistance Base[]

:   "*If Luke couldn't reach him, how could I?*"  
    "*Luke is a Jedi, you're his father.*"
:   ―Han and Leia[[1]](#cite_note-TFA-1)

 [![Leia, Han, C-3PO, and the Resistance leaders observe the recovered map.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/Resistance_Base_with_Map.png/revision/latest?cb=20160425034737) [![Leia, Han, C-3PO, and the Resistance leaders observe the recovered map.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/Resistance_Base_with_Map.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160425034737)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/Resistance_Base_with_Map.png/revision/latest?cb=20160425034737) 

Leia, Han, C-3PO, and the Resistance leaders observe the recovered map.

 

Han, Chewbacca, and Finn are brought to the Resistance base on [D'Qar](/wiki/D%27Qar "D'Qar"). BB-8 encounters the astromech droid R2-D2, who, as [C-3PO](/wiki/C-3PO "C-3PO") explains, has been dormant since Luke's disappearance. With the recovered map from BB-8 displayed on hologram, 3PO reveals that it is only partially complete, and that the map matches no charted system on record. It is revealed that Han and Leia are aware that their son is Kylo Ren, and that their son's fall to the dark side, despite Luke's efforts to guide him, caused them to separate, with Han returning to his smuggling business and Leia spearheading the activities of the Resistance.

Upon finding the location of the Resistance base, the Starkiller begins draining the power of the sun to destroy D'Qar. Meanwhile, the Resistance plans an attack of their own. Finn gives them the Starkiller's blueprints, which reveal that the Starkiller drains the energy of a star in order to charge its primary weapon, and that it requires a [thermal oscillator](/wiki/Thermal_oscillator "Thermal oscillator"), which sustains the energy on the planet, in order to function. If the thermal oscillator were destroyed, it would de-stabilize the planet's core and implode the base. However, they would need to do it before the First Order charges the Starkiller weapon and destroys D'Qar. Finn, Han, and Chewie volunteer to disable the base's defensive shield from the inside. Before departing to Starkiller Base, Han and Leia embrace, and Leia pleads Han to bring their son home.

### Rey's capture[]

:   "*You're afraid... that you will never be as strong as Darth Vader!*"
:   ―Rey to Kylo Ren[[1]](#cite_note-TFA-1)

Rey is brought to Starkiller Base and interrogated by Kylo Ren, who wants information on the map to Luke Skywalker. Ren takes off his helmet and shows her his face. Initially, Ren is able to see into Rey's mind, mentioning an island surrounded by water. However, the dark warrior has a difficult time probing her mind, and Rey is even able to push back into Ren's mind. After a mental struggle, Rey announces that she can sense fear in him - fear that he will never be as powerful as Darth Vader. Humiliated, Kylo storms out of the room to seek audience with Snoke.

 [![Rey uses a mind trick on a stormtrooper to aid her escape.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/89/Rey_and_Stormtrooper.png/revision/latest?cb=20200624103033) [![Rey uses a mind trick on a stormtrooper to aid her escape.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/89/Rey_and_Stormtrooper.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200624103033)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/89/Rey_and_Stormtrooper.png/revision/latest?cb=20200624103033) 

Rey uses a mind trick on a stormtrooper to aid her escape.

 

Left alone and aware of what just happened, Rey realizes it is as Kanata told her: she truly is [Force-sensitive](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive"). She attempts to use a Jedi [mind trick](/wiki/Mind_trick "Mind trick") on her [stormtrooper guard](/wiki/FN-1824 "FN-1824"), to make him release her and leave the door open. It doesn't work, but Rey tries again: this time he walks over and tells her he will tighten her restraints instead of undoing them. Concentrating, Rey tries one last time, and the stormtrooper listens to her demands. She quickly also remembers to have him drop his blaster as he leaves so she can arm herself. Rey then makes her way through Starkiller Base, honing her Force abilities while using stealth. She also draws on her experience climbing through wrecked Imperial starships to make her way through the bowels of the installation's machinery. Meanwhile, Kylo reveals to Snoke that Rey is strong with the Force but untrained, and Snoke commands Kylo to bring Rey to him. When Kylo discovers that Rey escaped, he throws another fit of rage, slashing at her empty restraint chair.

### [Battle of Starkiller Base](/wiki/Battle_of_Starkiller_Base "Battle of Starkiller Base")[]

 [![The battle over the trenches of Starkiller Base.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b7/Battle_of_Starkiller_Base.png/revision/latest?cb=20160416213048) [![The battle over the trenches of Starkiller Base.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b7/Battle_of_Starkiller_Base.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160416213048)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b7/Battle_of_Starkiller_Base.png/revision/latest?cb=20160416213048) 

The battle over the trenches of Starkiller Base.

 

Han Solo pilots the *Millennium Falcon* to Starkiller Base accompanied by Chewbacca and Finn. Finn's main objective is to rescue Rey from captivity. Since the Starkiller's shields have a fractional refresh rate, Han pilots through the shields at lightspeed, and the *Falcon* makes a rough landing at the edge of a cliff. Han, Chewbacca, and Finn sneak into the main base and capture Captain Phasma, whom they force to disable the shields before disposing of her in a [garbage chute](/wiki/Garbage_compactor "Garbage compactor"). They reunite with Rey, who had already escaped on her own. With the shields down, [Blue Squadron](/wiki/Blue_Squadron_(Resistance) "Blue Squadron (Resistance)") and [Red Squadron](/wiki/Red_Squadron_(Resistance) "Red Squadron (Resistance)") led by [Black Leader](/wiki/Black_Leader "Black Leader") Poe Dameron commence their assault. They fire on the Starkiller's hexagonal oscillator structure, but fail to destroy it as the First Order sends TIE fighters to stage a counterattack and throw the Resistance into chaos.

 [![Han attempts to convince his son to abandon the dark side.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4f/HanSoloAndSon.png/revision/latest?cb=20191005122058) [![Han attempts to convince his son to abandon the dark side.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4f/HanSoloAndSon.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20191005122058)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4f/HanSoloAndSon.png/revision/latest?cb=20191005122058) 

Han attempts to convince his son to abandon the dark side.

 

Seeing this, Han, Chewbacca, Finn, and Rey try to create an opening by planting thermal detonators inside the base. Sensing his father's presence, Kylo goes to meet Han. Han then confronts his son, Kylo Ren, calling to him by his birth name, "Ben". They approach each other on a bridge over a large pit, and Han pleads with his son to reject Snoke and return to the light side of the Force. Ben, removing his mask and seeming regretful and scared, holds out his lightsaber to Solo, asking for his father's help. Han replies that he would do anything for him, but when he tries to take the lightsaber from Ben's hand, he resists. Ben twists the angle of the hilt and ignites the weapon through Han's chest. Witnessed by Rey, Finn, and Chewbacca, Han strokes his son's face for the last time, before falling to his death. Enraged, Chewbacca, Rey, and Finn start firing at Ren and the stormtroopers. As the firefight rages, back on D'Qar Leia has to sit down when she feels Han die through the Force, squeezing her eyes shut against the tears. Chewbacca injures Ren with his bowcaster, but Ren chases them out of the base and catches up to Finn and Rey in the forest.

 [![Kylo Ren locks sabers with the former stormtrooper.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0d/Kylo_Ren_duels_Finn.png/revision/latest?cb=20160403173835) [![Kylo Ren locks sabers with the former stormtrooper.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0d/Kylo_Ren_duels_Finn.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160403173835)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0d/Kylo_Ren_duels_Finn.png/revision/latest?cb=20160403173835) 

Kylo Ren locks sabers with the former stormtrooper.

 

Rey calls Ren a monster and then proceeds to shoot him with her blaster, but Ren knocks Rey out by Force pushing her into a tree. A desperate and terrified Finn comes to her aid immediately. Ren angrily accuses Finn of being a traitor. Finn pulls out Luke's old lightsaber and attacks him in a rage. Ren is already badly injured, bleeding out of his abdomen from the bowcaster wound, but even so is too much for Finn. Finn manages to deal him a glancing wound, but nonetheless Ren quickly overpowers the former stormtrooper and deals him a grievous injury to his back. Ren tries to use [telekinesis](/wiki/Telekinesis "Telekinesis") to pick up the lightsaber his grandfather built, but it resists his pull and instead flies to Rey, who has awakened from her stupor.

 [![Poe flies in and destroys the Starkiller's thermal oscillator.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/Poe_blowing_up_Starkiller_Base.png/revision/latest?cb=20160304073507) [![Poe flies in and destroys the Starkiller's thermal oscillator.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/Poe_blowing_up_Starkiller_Base.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160304073507)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/Poe_blowing_up_Starkiller_Base.png/revision/latest?cb=20160304073507) 

Poe flies in and destroys the Starkiller's thermal oscillator.

 

During this time, Chewie activates the thermal detonators in the base, allowing Poe to lead a squadron of X-wings into the trenches of Starkiller Base. Poe finds an opening in the thermal oscillator and enters, while a following TIE crashes, unable to execute the same flight maneuver. Inside, Poe fires volley after volley of [torpedoes](/wiki/Proton_torpedo "Proton torpedo"), destroying the Starkiller's thermal oscillator thirty seconds before it finishes draining the sun to completely charge its primary weapon. A chain reaction is set off, destroying the base and levels the entire planet's terrain - without the weapon to dissipate it, the stored solar energy begins tearing the planet apart from the inside.

 [![Rey and Kylo Ren duel on Starkiller Base.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/01/Kylo_Ren_duels_Rey.png/revision/latest?cb=20200624100949) [![Rey and Kylo Ren duel on Starkiller Base.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/01/Kylo_Ren_duels_Rey.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200624100949)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/01/Kylo_Ren_duels_Rey.png/revision/latest?cb=20200624100949) 

Rey and Kylo Ren duel on Starkiller Base.

 

Rey and Ren continue fighting: Ren has taken even more wounds, from Chewbacca, Finn, and Rey, but even so initially holds the advantage, drawing on his rage to ignore the pain. Ren becomes so impressed with Rey that he tries to tempt her, complimenting her strength with the Force and offering to complete her training if she joins him. This backfires, however, as it only serves to reassure Rey of her own power, she begins to draw on the Force to hone her attacks, and the tide of the duel shifts. Ultimately, Rey is able to overpower Ren and deal him a severe wound to his face while severing his lightsaber in two. By this point, Kylo has taken too many wounds to continue standing, but he still struggles in vain to rise again. Before Rey can move in to finish him off, a large trench forms between them as the base begins to fall apart.

Rey returns to Finn, despairing that Finn is not waking up and that they are trapped on the rupturing planet. However, Chewbacca arrives with the *Millennium Falcon* to rescue them. Inside the main base, chaos reigns as General Hux has already fled, and the other officers rush to abandon the installation as well. Hux, meanwhile, reports to Snoke, who orders him to rescue Ren and flee the base, so Ren can finish his training. The *Millennium Falcon* and the remainder of the Resistance fleet manage to escape Starkiller Base as it erupts into a ball of fire, eventually forming a small star. They jump quickly to hyperspace and return to D'Qar.

### Locating Luke Skywalker[]

:   "*May the Force be with you.*"
:   ―Leia to Rey[[1]](#cite_note-TFA-1)

The Resistance celebrates their victory while Leia, Chewbacca, and Rey mourn Han's death. R2-D2 suddenly awakens and reveals that he holds the map to Luke's location, with the only piece of the map missing being the one BB-8 was given by Poe. Together they complete the map and reveal the location of [Ahch-To](/wiki/Ahch-To "Ahch-To"), the planet on which Luke Skywalker sought out the first Jedi Temple. As the unconscious Finn recovers in the medical unit, Rey kisses him on the head and thanks him for everything.

 [![Rey finds Luke Skywalker on the oceanic planet of Ahch-To.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/19/Luke_and_Rey_on_Ahch-To.png/revision/latest?cb=20250429051547) [![Rey finds Luke Skywalker on the oceanic planet of Ahch-To.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/19/Luke_and_Rey_on_Ahch-To.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250429051547)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/19/Luke_and_Rey_on_Ahch-To.png/revision/latest?cb=20250429051547) 

Rey finds Luke Skywalker on the oceanic planet of Ahch-To.

 

With R2-D2 and Chewbacca in tow, Rey leaves on the *Millennium Falcon* and follows the map to the distant planet, a water world dotted with islands, which she had previously seen in her visions. Rey pilots the starship to a [particular island](/wiki/Temple_Island "Temple Island") with a large, ancient [stone village](/wiki/Jedi_village "Jedi village") on it. She climbs the rock-carved steps to the [top of the island](/wiki/Saddle_(Ahch-To) "Saddle (Ahch-To)"), where she finds Luke Skywalker, with a grim look on his face. Both remain silent as Rey presents him with his father's lightsaber.

## Development[]

:   "*I keep telling J.J. Abrams this is a $4 billion movie. We need to treat this very special. It's an unbelievable privilege and unbelievable responsibility to take a jewel and treat it in a way that is respectful of its past but brings it into the future.*"
:   ―Bob Iger[[6]](#cite_note-Theme-6)

 [![The Disney acquisition of Lucasfilm from George Lucas paved the way for the creation of Star Wars: Episode VII.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/58/DisneyLucas.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20121113230240) [![The Disney acquisition of Lucasfilm from George Lucas paved the way for the creation of Star Wars: Episode VII.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/58/DisneyLucas.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20121113230240)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/58/DisneyLucas.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20121113230240) 

The Disney acquisition of Lucasfilm from George Lucas paved the way for the creation of *Star Wars*: Episode VII.

 

On [October 30](/wiki/October_30 "October 30"), [2012](/wiki/2012 "2012"), [The Walt Disney Company](/wiki/The_Walt_Disney_Company "The Walt Disney Company") announced that it had purchased [Lucasfilm](/wiki/Lucasfilm "Lucasfilm"), the production company behind the creation of the *[Star Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars "Star Wars")* franchise, from its owner, *Star Wars* creator [George Lucas](/wiki/George_Lucas "George Lucas"), for $4.05 billion.[[7]](#cite_note-Disney_press_release-7) The acquisition came in the wake of Lucas's announced retirement on [May 31](/wiki/May_31 "May 31"),[[8]](#cite_note-Paste_Magazine-8) and the subsequent [June 1](/wiki/June_1 "June 1") announcement that veteran film producer [Kathleen Kennedy](/wiki/Kathleen_Kennedy "Kathleen Kennedy") was succeeding Lucas as Lucasfilm's Co-Chair.[[9]](#cite_note-SW.com_-_Kathleen_Kennedy-9) As part of the merger, Disney revealed that it planned to produce a [sequel trilogy](/wiki/Sequel_trilogy "Sequel trilogy") of films beginning in [2015](/wiki/2015 "2015"), with Kennedy serving as executive producer.[[7]](#cite_note-Disney_press_release-7) Episode VII had already been in development for several months as of the Disney–Lucasfilm merger, and Lucas had written the story treatments for each of the three upcoming films.[[10]](#cite_note-The_Future_of_Star_Wars_Movies-10)

### Writing[]

:   "*J.J. and I sat down to do it under a lot of pressure, did the first draft quickly but then I've been writing it ever since! So that's almost two-and-a-half years that we've been writing the thing, and the thing that's never changed was the idea that there is a spirit to the original trilogy that we wanted to restore.*"
:   ―[Lawrence Kasdan](/wiki/Lawrence_Kasdan "Lawrence Kasdan"), in December 2015[[11]](#cite_note-Kasdan_Ghosts-11)

Lucasfilm confirmed on [November 9](/wiki/November_9 "November 9") that pre-production had begun on *Star Wars*: Episode VII, and that screenwriter [Michael Arndt](/wiki/Michael_Arndt "Michael Arndt") would write the script for the film.[[12]](#cite_note-Michael_Arndt-12) By this time, Arndt had already turned in a forty- to fifty-page story treatment[[13]](#cite_note-Vulture_-_Star_Wars:_Episode_VII_Writer_Confirmed-13)[[14]](#cite_note-Hollywood_Reporter_-_New_Star_Wars_Movie_Has_Treatment-14)[[15]](#cite_note-Hollywood_Reporter_-_Michael_Arndt_to_Write_Episode_VII-15) At some point, Lucas's story outlines were set aside,[[16]](#cite_note-Treatments_and_Lessons-16) and a writer's room of sorts was assembled at a [Santa Monica](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Santa_Monica,_California "wikipedia:Santa Monica, California") hotel. Those present included Arndt (still writing the script), [Kiri Hart](/wiki/Kiri_Hart "Kiri Hart"), [Lawrence Kasdan](/wiki/Lawrence_Kasdan "Lawrence Kasdan"), [Kathleen Kennedy](/wiki/Kathleen_Kennedy "Kathleen Kennedy") and [Simon Kinberg](/wiki/Simon_Kinberg "Simon Kinberg").[[17]](#cite_note-Kasdan-NYT-17)[[18]](#cite_note-18)[[11]](#cite_note-Kasdan_Ghosts-11) According to Kasdan, the sessions went on for months with little progress.[[17]](#cite_note-Kasdan-NYT-17) Abrams later described them as "a ton of ideas and outlines, a lot of cards on the wall, a lot of writing on whiteboards."[[19]](#cite_note-Genesis-19) Lucas was asked to be a consultant,[[7]](#cite_note-Disney_press_release-7) but he stepped away due to Disney's decision to take the story in a different direction than his original outlines.[[20]](#cite_note-20)[[21]](#cite_note-DisneyRejection-21) He later elaborated in an interview with [Stephen Colbert](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stephen_Colbert "wikipedia:Stephen Colbert"): "The original saga was about the father, the children, and the grandchildren. I don't think that's a secret to anybody—that's in the novels—and the children were in their 20s and everything. But they've taken it in a different direction, and I'm excited—they didn't use my story, so I don't know what they're doing."[[22]](#cite_note-22)

Arndt worked on the script throughout 2013.[[23]](#cite_note-Team_Scrambling-23) Arndt was told to focus on the female lead, but he had difficulty balancing this with the prominence of Luke, so the creative team decided to remove Luke from most of the film and make him the character everyone was looking for.[[24]](#cite_note-EWR2-24) Eventually, Arndt was let go, and Kasdan was asked to co-write the script with [J.J. Abrams](/wiki/J.J._Abrams "J.J. Abrams") (who had been announced as the film's director[[25]](#cite_note-JJConfirmed-25)), for which they were allowed creative freedom to come up with a story.[[26]](#cite_note-KasdanAbrams-26) In November 2013, Abrams and Kasdan started a new script, incorporating ideas that they each liked from the think tank. As Abrams told *Vanity Fair*, "We said, Blank page. Page one. What do we desperately want to see?"[[19]](#cite_note-Genesis-19) Referring to the writer's room sessions, Kasdan told craveonline.com "…for nine months you talk about something, and then you go off and start from scratch again. You don't flush, you know?"[[11]](#cite_note-Kasdan_Ghosts-11) Their writing process involved meeting up at cafes and restaurants and going on long walks through various major cities around the world—during which Abrams recorded their conversations on his phone.[[27]](#cite_note-Walk-27)[[19]](#cite_note-Genesis-19) They had put together a script by January 2014, though they were still working on major story elements even after production began that May.[[19]](#cite_note-Genesis-19) They were under pressure to deliver a script in a relatively short period of time, and some of the higher-ups reportedly requested that the film be delayed into 2016.[[23]](#cite_note-Team_Scrambling-23) (Kennedy was among those who objected to the original May 2015 release date.[[19]](#cite_note-Genesis-19)) Kasdan's son [Jon](/wiki/Jon_Kasdan "Jon Kasdan") had uncredited writing contributions to the script,[[28]](#cite_note-SW-A_Portrait_of_the_Scoundrel_as_a_Young_Man:_Writers_Lawrence_and_Jonathan_Kasdan_on_Solo:_A_Star_Wars_Story-28) and Episode VIII director [Rian Johnson](/wiki/Rian_Johnson "Rian Johnson") requested Abrams change the ending by having R2-D2 (not BB-8) come to Ahch-To and for Luke not to be floating boulders as originally intended.[[29]](#cite_note-29)[[30]](#cite_note-30)

### Production[]

:   "*I've learned to be very careful about* Star Wars*. If I say, 'There will be no skateboards in* Star Wars*'... that gets headlines.*"
:   ―Alan Horn, Disney Chairman[[31]](#cite_note-AlanHorn-31)

 [![The cast of Star Wars: The Force Awakens](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/86/Episode_7_Cast.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161017235319) [![The cast of Star Wars: The Force Awakens](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/86/Episode_7_Cast.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20161017235319)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/86/Episode_7_Cast.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161017235319) 

The cast of *Star Wars: The Force Awakens*

 

*The Force Awakens* began preliminary shooting in April 2014,[[32]](#cite_note-32)[[33]](#cite_note-33) with second-unit work taking place in [Iceland](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Iceland "wikipedia:Iceland") and [Abu Dhabi](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Abu_Dhabi "wikipedia:Abu Dhabi").[[34]](#cite_note-34)[[35]](#cite_note-35)[[36]](#cite_note-36) On [April 25](/wiki/April_25 "April 25"), Lucasfilm announced their plans for a new continuity that excluded the existing Expanded Universe, and confirmed that Episode VII and its sequels would not adhere to any existing continuity.[[37]](#cite_note-Canon_Announcement-37) This was followed on [April 29](/wiki/April_29 "April 29") by the official release of the cast list for the movie. Mark Hamill, Carrie Fisher, Harrison Ford, [Kenny Baker](/wiki/Kenny_Baker "Kenny Baker"), [Peter Mayhew](/wiki/Peter_Mayhew "Peter Mayhew"), and [Anthony Daniels](/wiki/Anthony_Daniels "Anthony Daniels") would return to reprise their roles as the main characters of the original trilogy, and they would be joined by a number of new actors in leading roles: [John Boyega](/wiki/John_Boyega "John Boyega"), [Daisy Ridley](/wiki/Daisy_Ridley "Daisy Ridley"), [Adam Driver](/wiki/Adam_Driver "Adam Driver"), [Oscar Isaac](/wiki/Oscar_Isaac "Oscar Isaac"), [Andy Serkis](/wiki/Andy_Serkis "Andy Serkis"), [Domhnall Gleeson](/wiki/Domhnall_Gleeson "Domhnall Gleeson"), and [Max von Sydow](/wiki/Max_von_Sydow "Max von Sydow").[[38]](#cite_note-Cast-38) Hamill remarked on returning to *Star Wars*: "Part of the experience of [*Star Wars*] in my life was coming down from that, putting it behind me. We had a beginning, middle, and an end. And I certainly, in a million years, never expected to return. I thought, even if they do more trilogies, my story is over."[[39]](#cite_note-39) [Denis Lawson](/wiki/Denis_Lawson "Denis Lawson") was asked to reprise his role as [Wedge Antilles](/wiki/Wedge_Antilles "Wedge Antilles") from the [original trilogy](/wiki/Original_trilogy "Original trilogy"), but declined, initially stating that it would have "bored" him,[[40]](#cite_note-40) but later claiming that he had been busy on another project.[[41]](#cite_note-41)

Principal photography was announced on [May 10](/wiki/May_10 "May 10"), 2013, and began on [May 16](/wiki/May_16 "May 16"), 2014 at the [UK's](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_Kingdom "wikipedia:United Kingdom") [Pinewood Studios](/wiki/Pinewood_Studios "Pinewood Studios").[[42]](#cite_note-UKprod-42)[[43]](#cite_note-Set_to_Roll-43)[[44]](#cite_note-FB_Prod_Began-44)[[45]](#cite_note-FB_Pinewood_Prod-45) For visual inspiration, Abrams looked at films directed by [John Ford](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Ford "wikipedia:John Ford"), [Akira Kurosawa](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Akira_Kurosawa "wikipedia:Akira Kurosawa"), and [Terrence Malick](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Terence_Malick "wikipedia:Terence Malick").[[46]](#cite_note-46) [Daniel Mindel](/wiki/Daniel_Mindel "Daniel Mindel")—who had previously worked with Abrams as director of photography—returned to collaborate with the director on the film.[[47]](#cite_note-47) Reportedly, one sequence was shot with [IMAX](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IMAX "wikipedia:IMAX") cameras.[[48]](#cite_note-48)[[49]](#cite_note-49) Although Peter Mayhew was able to reprise the role as Chewbacca,[[50]](#cite_note-50) some scenes had to be shot with a stunt double, due to Mayhew's age and physical health.[[51]](#cite_note-51) On June 11, the 71-year old Harrison Ford broke his left leg when a hydraulic door at Pinewood Studios fell down and hit him, and was airlifted to John Radcliffe Hospital in Oxford.[[52]](#cite_note-52) His recovery forced him to drop out of filming for eight weeks.[[53]](#cite_note-53) Abrams also sustained a minor back injury when he tried to help lift the door off of Ford's leg.[[54]](#cite_note-54) On June 28, actor Andy Serkis confirmed that [The Imaginarium Studios](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Imaginarium_Studios "wikipedia:The Imaginarium Studios") would be involved with performance capture on the film, as well as all future *Star Wars* projects. Serkis also confirmed that the character he plays in the film would utilize performance capture.[[55]](#cite_note-55) On July 6, Lucasfilm confirmed that actors [Crystal Clarke](/wiki/Crystal_Clarke "Crystal Clarke") and [Pip Andersen](/wiki/Pip_Andersen "Pip Andersen") were cast in the film through open casting calls in the United Kingdom. They also revealed that production would take a two-week hiatus in August to accommodate Harrison Ford's leg injury. Afterwards shooting would resume, and conclude later in the fall.[[56]](#cite_note-Production_Update-56)

On [November 6](/wiki/November_6 "November 6"), 2014, the official *Star Wars* Twitter account announced that the film had completed principal photography. The post gave the official title for the film as *Star Wars: The Force Awakens*, and was accompanied by a title card for the new name that, like the original trilogy, excluded the "Episode" subtitle.[[57]](#cite_note-Force_Awakens_Twitter-57) The film had gone through several titles, including *Shadow of the Empire*, similar to [*Shadows of the Empire*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Shadows_of_the_Empire "Star Wars: Shadows of the Empire").[[58]](#cite_note-58)[[59]](#cite_note-59)

### Design[]

[Michael Kaplan](/wiki/Michael_Kaplan "Michael Kaplan"), who had designed the costumes for Abrams' *Star Trek* films, also signed on to costume Episode VII.[[60]](#cite_note-60) Kaplan designed new stormtrooper uniforms for the film, as it was determined that the original costumes would not stand up to modern scrutiny. These new uniforms were inspired by [Apple](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Apple_Inc. "wikipedia:Apple Inc.") products.[[61]](#cite_note-61) The production team built a new C-3PO suit to accommodate Anthony Daniels,[[62]](#cite_note-62) while the [R2-D2](/wiki/R2-D2 "R2-D2") model was provided and overseen by members of the [R2-D2 Builders Club](/wiki/R2-D2_Builders_Club "R2-D2 Builders Club").[[63]](#cite_note-R2_in_Episode_VII-63)

Supervising sound editor [Matthew Wood](/wiki/Matthew_Wood "Matthew Wood") brought in former cast and crew members of *[Star Wars: The Clone Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars "Star Wars: The Clone Wars")* to record various background dialogue.[[64]](#cite_note-64) [Ewan McGregor](/wiki/Ewan_McGregor "Ewan McGregor") and [Frank Oz](/wiki/Frank_Oz "Frank Oz") also recorded new lines for the scene of Rey's Force vision. McGregor's recording was combined with audio of the late [Alec Guinness](/wiki/Alec_Guinness "Alec Guinness"), and pre-existing Yoda audio was ultimately used in lieu of Oz's new recording.[[65]](#cite_note-65)

### Music[]

During a concert with the Young Musician's Foundation Debut Orchestra on [February 9](/wiki/February_9 "February 9"), 2013 composer [John Williams](/wiki/John_Williams "John Williams") stated that he was hoping to get the chance to write the [musical scores](/wiki/Musical_score "Musical score") for the new trilogy.[[66]](#cite_note-66) Abrams made further statements on this at a *[Star Trek Into Darkness](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Star_Trek_Into_Darkness "wikipedia:Star Trek Into Darkness")* conference on April 29, stating, "Again, for Star Wars, it's very early days, but I believe that, going forward, John Williams will be doing that film because he was there long before I was."[[67]](#cite_note-67) On [July 27](/wiki/July_27 "July 27"), 2013, a video of Williams confirming he would score the new film was screened at *Star Wars* [Celebration Europe II](/wiki/Celebration_Europe_II "Celebration Europe II").[[68]](#cite_note-John_Williams-68) On [March 21](/wiki/March_21 "March 21"), 2015, Lucasfilm revealed that John Williams would conduct the score for *The Force Awakens* in Los Angeles. Williams's previous *Star Wars* scores were recorded in the United Kingdom with the London Symphony Orchestra.[[69]](#cite_note-Symphony-69) The sessions lasted from summer through fall of 2015.[[70]](#cite_note-70)

## Release and reception[]

:   "*We're living in such a different age now. It's like a competition to see who can leak information faster than the next guy. I don't get it. I'm keeping my fingers crossed that they don't get a copy of the script and leak the whole thing on the Internet.*"
:   ―Mark Hamill[[71]](#cite_note-HamillLeak-71)

 [![Official logo](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/Star_Wars_The_Force_Awakens.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150504052358) [![Official logo](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/Star_Wars_The_Force_Awakens.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150504052358)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/Star_Wars_The_Force_Awakens.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150504052358) 

Official logo

 

The first teaser trailer—released early due to both fan demand and Abrams' request[[6]](#cite_note-Theme-6)[[72]](#cite_note-72)—was announced via the [Bad Robot Productions](/wiki/Bad_Robot_Productions "Bad Robot Productions") Twitter account, with a note from Abrams saying fans will see a "tiny peek at what we're working on."[[73]](#cite_note-Teaser_Confirmed-73) The 88-second teaser premiered in 30 theaters across North America and was released online on [November 28](/wiki/November_28 "November 28"), 2014.[[74]](#cite_note-SW.com_Trailer_Tease-74)[[75]](#cite_note-TFA_Teaser-75) The teaser was shown in theaters around the world beginning in December 2014.[[74]](#cite_note-SW.com_Trailer_Tease-74) Character names were revealed shortly thereafter in online mock collector cards.[[76]](#cite_note-76) Earlier that November, J.J. Abrams made a cameo on *[Last Week Tonight with John Oliver](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Last_Week_Tonight_with_John_Oliver "wikipedia:Last Week Tonight with John Oliver")*, in which he could be seen directing R2-D2 on the set of *The Force Awakens*. When a fish from Oliver's salmon cannon falls on the script that he's holding, Abrams gets frustrated and quits the film.[[77]](#cite_note-77)

A second teaser was released on [April 16](/wiki/April_16 "April 16"), 2015.[[78]](#cite_note-SWYouTube-Star_Wars:_The_Force_Awakens_Official_Teaser_#2-78) The June 2015 issue of *Variety* featured a cover story on *The Force Awakens*, with interviews with cast and crew and images from an [Annie Leibovitz](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Annie_Leibovitz "wikipedia:Annie Leibovitz") photo shoot.[[79]](#cite_note-Vanity_Fair_cover-79) The August 2015 issues of *[Entertainment Weekly](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Entertainment_Weekly "wikipedia:Entertainment Weekly")* and *[Empire](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Empire_(film_magazine) "wikipedia:Empire (film magazine)")* also had the film as their cover stories.[[80]](#cite_note-SW-Entertainment_Weekly_Previews_Star_Wars:_The_Force_Awakens-80)[[81]](#cite_note-81)[[82]](#cite_note-82) *The Force Awakens* had a presence at 2015's [San Diego Comic-Con](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/San_Diego_Comic-Con_International "wikipedia:San Diego Comic-Con International") and [D23](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Disney_D23 "wikipedia:Disney D23") events.[[83]](#cite_note-SW-Star_Wars:_The_Force_Awakens_and_More_Coming_to_San_Diego_Comic-Con_2015-83)[[84]](#cite_note-SW-8_Cool_Star_Wars_Things_at_D23_Expo-84) At the latter, it was revealed that [Drew Struzan](/wiki/Drew_Struzan "Drew Struzan") had returned to create poster art for the film, including a poster exclusive to the event.[[85]](#cite_note-85) A third, shorter teaser was released on the *Star Wars* [Instagram](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Instagram "wikipedia:Instagram") on [August 27](/wiki/August_27 "August 27").[[86]](#cite_note-SW-New_Footage_of_Star_Wars:_The_Force_Awakens_Debuts_on_Instagram!-86) On [September 23](/wiki/September_23 "September 23"), [Facebook](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Facebook "wikipedia:Facebook") released a 360-degree panoramic video clip of a speeder driving across Jakku.[[87]](#cite_note-87) The official [one sheet](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/One_sheet "wikipedia:One sheet") was released on [October 18](/wiki/October_18 "October 18"), 2015,[[88]](#cite_note-Poster-88) while the full-length trailer debuted on [October 19](/wiki/October_19 "October 19") with [ESPN's](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ESPN "wikipedia:ESPN") [Monday Night Football](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Monday_Night_Football "wikipedia:Monday Night Football").[[89]](#cite_note-89)

The cast and crew appeared on various TV programs, including *[Good Morning America](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Good_Morning_America "wikipedia:Good Morning America")*,[[90]](#cite_note-90) *[Live! with Kelly and Michael](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Live!_with_Kelly_and_Michael "wikipedia:Live! with Kelly and Michael")*,[[91]](#cite_note-91) and *[60 Minutes](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/60_Minutes "wikipedia:60 Minutes")*.[[92]](#cite_note-92)[[93]](#cite_note-93) Abrams, Boyega, and Ridley participated in a *[Saturday Night Live](/wiki/Saturday_Night_Live "Saturday Night Live")* sketch featuring cast members and guest celebrities in a series of fake auditions. Among the subjects parodied were racist reactions to Boyega's casting, Lucas's comments about not being involved, and Abrams's involvement in the rival franchise *Star Trek*.[[94]](#cite_note-94)[[95]](#cite_note-95) (More of these later aired on June 1, 2016.[[96]](#cite_note-96)) Abrams and the cast appeared on a *Star Wars*–themed episode of *[Jimmy Kimmel Live!](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jimmy_Kimmel_Live! "wikipedia:Jimmy Kimmel Live!")* on [November 23](/wiki/November_23 "November 23").[[97]](#cite_note-97) Harrison Ford spoke about his injury during shooting on *The Tonight Show with Jimmy Fallon* by destroying a Han Solo action figure.[[98]](#cite_note-98)

Some members of the cast and crew also participated in an official press conference on [December 5](/wiki/December_5 "December 5").[[99]](#cite_note-99) The film had its [red-carpet](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Red_carpet "wikipedia:Red carpet") premiere on [December 14](/wiki/December_14 "December 14") at [Hollywood Boulevard](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hollywood_Boulevard "wikipedia:Hollywood Boulevard").[[100]](#cite_note-100) The event was streamed live on StarWars.com.[[101]](#cite_note-SW-Watch_the_Star_Wars:_The_Force_Awakens_Red_Carpet_Live_at_StarWars.com-101) The cast (including the droids) participated in an a [cappella](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A_cappella "wikipedia:A cappella") [medley](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medley_(music) "wikipedia:Medley (music)") of the music from the series with Jimmy Fallon and The Roots on *The Tonight Show*.[[102]](#cite_note-102) Ford and Abrams participated on a sketch on *The Late Show with Stephen Colbert* depicting what convinced Ford to return: Colbert allegedly almost convinced Abrams to recast the role of Han with him.[[103]](#cite_note-103) Later, when he appeared on *Conan*, he was asked to sign producer Jordan Schlansky's LEGO *Millennium Falcon* and "accidentally" dropped it.[[104]](#cite_note-104) Abrams made a cameo on a May 2016 episode of *[The Late Late Show with James Corden](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Late_Late_Show_with_James_Corden "wikipedia:The Late Late Show with James Corden")*, in which he appeared in the backseat of a car and directed "Chewbacca Mom" [Candace Payne](/wiki/Candace_Payne "Candace Payne") on how to properly use a Chewbacca mask.[[105]](#cite_note-105)

### Charity[]

On May 21, 2014, Disney, Lucasfilm, and Bad Robot announced "Force for Change," a charity campaign "dedicated to finding creative solutions to some of the world's biggest problems"; initially, the campaign was focused on contributing to [UNICEF](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/UNICEF "wikipedia:UNICEF"). Each person who donated was entered to win a set visit to and appearance in Episode VII.[[106]](#cite_note-106) On [August 11](/wiki/August_11 "August 11"), Denver, Colorado resident [D.C. Barns](/wiki/D.C._Barns "D.C. Barns") was announced as the contest's winner.[[107]](#cite_note-Barns-107) J.J. Abrams later released a YouTube video in which he announced that the contest had raised $4.26 million.[[108]](#cite_note-108) In August 2014, several of the film's cast and crew participated in the "[Ice Bucket Challenge](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ice_Bucket_challenge "wikipedia:Ice Bucket challenge")," an Internet phenomenon whereby one pours water onto one's head as a pledge to donate to the [ALS association](http://www.alsa.org/fight-als/ice-bucket-challenge.html).[[109]](#cite_note-109) On April 21, 2015, Abrams appeared on *Jimmy Kimmel Live!*, where he performed the "Twizzler challenge" with Chewbacca, in honor of Autism Awareness Month.[[110]](#cite_note-110) In August 2015, Lucasfilm and HP began a two-month program called "Art Awakens," in which people submitted art inspired by *The Force Awakens*, of which a certain number were chosen for an art exhibit, the proceeds of which went to "Force for Change."[[111]](#cite_note-SW-Lucasfilm_and_HP_Celebrate_Star_Wars:_The_Force_Awakens_with_Art_Awakens_Program-111) On November 5, 2015, director J.J. Abrams screened an unfinished version of the film for [Daniel Fleetwood](/wiki/Daniel_Fleetwood "Daniel Fleetwood"), a 32-year-old *Star Wars* fan with an aggressive form of cancer, who was likely to die before the film's release. The campaign for him to see the film was supported by several of the film's stars, including John Boyega, Mark Hamill, and Gwendoline Christie.
